                               FirstLineHasBeenOutput := FALSE;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  CurrencyExchangeRate@1000 : Record 330;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW THEN
                                    CODEUNIT.RUN(CODEUNIT::"Sales Cr. Memo-Printed",Header);

                                  CurrReport.LANGUAGE := Language.GetLanguageID("Language Code");

                                  FormatAddressFields(Header);
                                  FormatDocumentFields(Header);

                                  IF NOT Cust.GET("Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
                                    CLEAR(Cust);

                                  IF "Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    CurrencyExchangeRate.FindCurrency("Posting Date","Currency Code",1);
                                    CalculatedExchRate :=
                                      ROUND(1 / "Currency Factor" * CurrencyExchangeRate."Exchange Rate Amount",0.000001);
                                    ExchangeRateText := STRSUBSTNO(ExchangeRateTxt,CalculatedExchRate,CurrencyExchangeRate."Exchange Rate Amount");
                                  END;

                                  IF LogInteraction AND NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW THEN BEGIN
                                    IF "Bill-to Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                      SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                        6,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Contact,"Bill-to Contact No.","Salesperson Code",
                                        "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'')
                                    ELSE
                                      SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                        6,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Customer,"Bill-to Customer No.","Salesperson Code",
                                        "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'');
                                        Cust.GET(Header."Bill-to Customer No.");
                                      signDocument(Header .GETFILTER("No."),Cust.TIN, Cust."Exemption Number");
                                  END;

                                  TotalSubTotal := 0;
                                  TotalInvDiscAmount := 0;
                                  TotalAmount := 0;
                                  TotalAmountVAT := 0;
                                  TotalAmountInclVAT := 0;
                                  TotalPaymentDiscOnVAT := 0;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Sell-to Customer No.,No. Printed }

    { 1570;1   ;DataItem;Line                ;
               DataItemTable=Table115;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document No.,Line No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               VATAmountLine.DELETEALL;
                               VATClauseLine.DELETEALL;
                               ShipmentLine.RESET;
                               ShipmentLine.DELETEALL;
                               MoreLines := FIND('+');
                               WHILE MoreLines AND (Description = '') AND ("No." = '') AND (Quantity = 0) AND (Amount = 0) DO
                                 MoreLines := NEXT(-1) <> 0;
                               IF NOT MoreLines THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               SETRANGE("Line No.",0,"Line No.");
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS("Line Amount",Amount,"Amount Including VAT","Inv. Discount Amount");
                               TransHeaderAmount := 0;
                               PrevLineAmount := 0;
                               FirstLineHasBeenOutput := FALSE;
                               CompanyInfo.CALCFIELDS(Picture);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  PostedShipmentDate := 0D;
                                  IF Quantity <> 0 THEN
                                    PostedShipmentDate := FindPostedShipmentDate;
                                  IF GLAccount.GET(Line."No.") THEN
                                    HSCode := GLAccount."HS Codes";
                                  IF Type = Type::"G/L Account" THEN
                                    "No." := '';

                                  IF "Line Discount %" = 0 THEN
                                    LineDiscountPctText := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    LineDiscountPctText := STRSUBSTNO('%1%',-ROUND("Line Discount %",0.1));

                                  VATAmountLine.INIT;
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT Identifier" := "VAT Identifier";
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT Calculation Type" := "VAT Calculation Type";
                                  VATAmountLine."Tax Group Code" := "Tax Group Code";
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT %" := "VAT %";
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT Base" := Amount;
                                  VATAmountLine."Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
                                  VATAmountLine."Line Amount" := "Line Amount";
                                  IF "Allow Invoice Disc." THEN
                                    VATAmountLine."Inv. Disc. Base Amount" := "Line Amount";
                                  VATAmountLine."Invoice Discount Amount" := "Inv. Discount Amount";
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT Clause Code" := "VAT Clause Code";
                                  IF ("VAT %" <> 0) OR ("VAT Clause Code" <> '') OR (Amount <> "Amount Including VAT") THEN
                                    VATAmountLine.InsertLine;

                                  TransHeaderAmount += PrevLineAmount;
                                  PrevLineAmount := "Line Amount";
                                  TotalSubTotal += "Line Amount";
                                  TotalInvDiscAmount -= "Inv. Discount Amount";
                                  TotalAmount += Amount;
                                  TotalAmountVAT += "Amount Including VAT" - Amount;
                                  TotalAmountInclVAT += "Amount Including VAT";
                                  TotalPaymentDiscOnVAT += -("Line Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount" - "Amount Including VAT");

                                  IF FirstLineHasBeenOutput THEN
                                    CLEAR(CompanyInfo.Picture);
                                  FirstLineHasBeenOutput := TRUE;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Header;
               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 6558;1   ;DataItem;VATAmountLine       ;
               DataItemTable=Table290;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(VAT Identifier,VAT Calculation Type,Tax Group Code,Use Tax,Positive);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(
                                 "Line Amount","Inv. Disc. Base Amount",
                                 "Invoice Discount Amount","VAT Base","VAT Amount",
                                 VATBaseLCY,VATAmountLCY);

                               TotalVATBaseLCY := 0;
                               TotalVATAmountLCY := 0;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  VATBaseLCY :=
                                    GetBaseLCY(
                                      Header."Posting Date",Header."Currency Code",
                                      Header."Currency Factor");
                                  VATAmountLCY :=
                                    GetAmountLCY(
                                      Header."Posting Date",Header."Currency Code",
                                      Header."Currency Factor");

                                  TotalVATBaseLCY += VATBaseLCY;
                                  TotalVATAmountLCY += VATAmountLCY;

                                  IF "VAT Clause Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    VATClauseLine := VATAmountLine;
                                    IF VATClauseLine.INSERT THEN;
                                  END;
                                END;

               Temporary=Yes }

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitLogInteraction@1();
    BEGIN
      LogInteraction := SegManagement.FindInteractTmplCode(6) <> '';
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FindPostedShipmentDate@6() : Date;
    VAR
      ReturnReceiptHeader@1000 : Record 6660;
      SalesShipmentBuffer2@1001 : Record 7190;
    BEGIN
      IF Line."Return Receipt No." <> '' THEN
        IF ReturnReceiptHeader.GET(Line."Return Receipt No.") THEN
          EXIT(ReturnReceiptHeader."Posting Date");
      IF Header."Return Order No." = '' THEN
        EXIT(Header."Posting Date");
      IF Line.Type = Line.Type::" " THEN
        EXIT(0D);

      ShipmentLine.GetLinesForSalesCreditMemoLine(Line,Header);

      ShipmentLine.RESET;
      ShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Line No." ,Line."Line No.");
      IF ShipmentLine.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        SalesShipmentBuffer2 := ShipmentLine;
        IF NOT DisplayShipmentInformation THEN
          IF ShipmentLine.NEXT = 0 THEN BEGIN
            ShipmentLine.GET(
              SalesShipmentBuffer2."Document No.",SalesShipmentBuffer2."Line No.",SalesShipmentBuffer2."Entry No.");
            ShipmentLine.DELETE;
            EXIT(SalesShipmentBuffer2."Posting Date");
          END;
        ShipmentLine.CALCSUMS(Quantity);
        IF ShipmentLine.Quantity <> Line.Quantity THEN BEGIN
          ShipmentLine.DELETEALL;
          EXIT(Header."Posting Date");
        END;
      END;
      EXIT(Header."Posting Date");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DocumentCaption@4() : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      IF Header."Prepayment Credit Memo" THEN
        EXIT(SalesPrepCreditMemoNoLbl);
      EXIT(SalesCreditMemoNoLbl);
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitializeRequest@5(NewLogInteraction@1002 : Boolean;DisplayAsmInfo@1003 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      LogInteraction := NewLogInteraction;
      DisplayAssemblyInformation := DisplayAsmInfo;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetUOMText@12(UOMCode@1000 : Code[10]) : Text[10];
    VAR
      UnitOfMeasure@1001 : Record 204;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT UnitOfMeasure.GET(UOMCode) THEN
        EXIT(UOMCode);
      EXIT(UnitOfMeasure.Description);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateReportTotalLines@15();
    BEGIN
      ReportTotalsLine.DELETEALL;
      IF (TotalInvDiscAmount <> 0) OR (TotalAmountVAT <> 0) THEN
        ReportTotalsLine.Add(SubtotalLbl,TotalSubTotal,TRUE,FALSE,FALSE);
      IF TotalInvDiscAmount <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        ReportTotalsLine.Add(InvDiscountAmtLbl,TotalInvDiscAmount,FALSE,FALSE,FALSE);
        IF TotalAmountVAT <> 0 THEN
          ReportTotalsLine.Add(TotalExclVATText,TotalAmount,TRUE,FALSE,FALSE);
      END;
      IF TotalAmountVAT <> 0 THEN
        ReportTotalsLine.Add(VATAmountLine.VATAmountText,TotalAmountVAT,FALSE,TRUE,FALSE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FormatAddressFields@2(VAR SalesCrMemoHeader@1000 : Record 114);
    BEGIN
      FormatAddr.GetCompanyAddr(SalesCrMemoHeader."Responsibility Center",RespCenter,CompanyInfo,CompanyAddr);
      FormatAddr.SalesCrMemoBillTo(CustAddr,SalesCrMemoHeader);
      ShowShippingAddr := FormatAddr.SalesCrMemoShipTo(ShipToAddr,CustAddr,SalesCrMemoHeader);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FormatDocumentFields@3(SalesCrMemoHeader@1000 : Record 114);
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesCrMemoHeader DO BEGIN
        FormatDocument.SetTotalLabels("Currency Code",TotalText,TotalInclVATText,TotalExclVATText);
        FormatDocument.SetSalesPerson(SalespersonPurchaser,"Salesperson Code",SalesPersonText);
        FormatDocument.SetPaymentTerms(PaymentTerms,"Payment Terms Code","Language Code");
        FormatDocument.SetPaymentMethod(PaymentMethod,"Payment Method Code");
        FormatDocument.SetShipmentMethod(ShipmentMethod,"Shipment Method Code","Language Code");

        FormatDocument.SetText("Applies-to Doc. No." <> '',STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',FORMAT("Applies-to Doc. Type"),"Applies-to Doc. No."));
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE signDocument@14(invoiceNumber@1000 : Code[50];tin@1018 : Code[50];exceptionNo@1019 : Code[50]);
    VAR
      invoice_number@1013 : Code[100];
      cu_serial_number@1012 : Code[100];
      cu_invoice_number@1011 : Code[100];
      verify_url@1010 : Text;
      salesinvoice@1008 : Record 114;
      JsonOut@1007 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.String";
      saleinvoiceline@1006 : Record 115;
      variables@1005 : Text;
      kradevices@1004 : Record 2000000130;
      InventoryPostingGroup@1003 : Record 94;
      Item@1002 : Record 27;
      customer@1001 : Record 18;
      KRAPrintLog@1009 : Record 99999;
      JSONTextWriter@1017 : DotNet "'Newtonsoft.Json, Version=6.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=30ad4fe6b2a6aeed'.Newtonsoft.Json.JsonTextWriter";
      JSON@1016 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.String";
      StringWriter@1015 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.IO.StringWriter";
      StringBuilder@1014 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Text.StringBuilder";
      HSCode2@1020 : Code[80];
      KRAPrintLog2@1021 : Record 99999;
      DetailedCustLedgEntry@1023 : Record 379;
      customerLedgerEntry@1022 : Record 21;
    BEGIN
      IF kradevices.GET(TRUE, kradevices."Device Type"::TIMS) THEN BEGIN
      //Get invoice

            KRAPrintLog.RESET;
      KRAPrintLog.SETRANGE("Document No", invoiceNumber);
      IF NOT KRAPrintLog.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN


      salesinvoice.GET(Header.GETFILTER("No."));
      IF salesinvoice."Applies-to Doc. No." <>'' THEN BEGIN
      StringBuilder:=StringBuilder.StringBuilder;
      StringWriter:=StringWriter.StringWriter(StringBuilder);
      JSONTextWriter:=JSONTextWriter.JsonTextWriter(StringWriter);
      JSONTextWriter.WriteStartObject;
      salesinvoice.CALCFIELDS(Amount, "Amount Including VAT");
      CreateJsonAttribute('invoice_date', salesinvoice."Document Date");
      CreateJsonAttribute('invoice_number', salesinvoice."No.");
      CreateJsonAttribute('invoice_pin', CompanyInfo."PIN NO.");
      CreateJsonAttribute('customer_pin', tin);
      CreateJsonAttribute('customer_exid', '');

      CreateJsonAttribute('grand_total', salesinvoice."Amount Including VAT");
      CreateJsonAttribute('rel_doc_number', salesinvoice."Applies-to Doc. No.");
      CreateJsonAttribute('tax_total', salesinvoice."Amount Including VAT"-salesinvoice.Amount);

      CreateJsonAttribute('sel_currency', 'KSH');

      JSONTextWriter.WritePropertyName('items_list');
      JSONTextWriter.WriteStartArray;
        saleinvoiceline.RESET;
        saleinvoiceline.SETRANGE("Document No.", salesinvoice."No.");
        saleinvoiceline.SETRANGE(Type, saleinvoiceline.Type::Item);
        IF saleinvoiceline.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
          // MESSAGE(FORMAT(salesinvoice."Prices Including VAT"));
          IF salesinvoice."Prices Including VAT"=TRUE THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
          IF GLAccount.GET(saleinvoiceline."No.") THEN
             HSCode2 := GLAccount."HS Codes";
            IF HSCode2 <> '' THEN
            JSONTextWriter.WriteValue(HSCode2+' '+saleinvoiceline.Description+' '+saleinvoiceline."Unit of Measure Code"+' '+FORMAT(saleinvoiceline.Quantity*1.0)+' '
            +FORMAT(ROUND((saleinvoiceline."Unit Price"), 0.0001, '>')*1.0)+'.0000'+' '+FORMAT(saleinvoiceline."Line Discount Amount")+'.0000'+
            ' '+FORMAT((saleinvoiceline."Amount Including VAT"))+'.0000')
            ELSE
              JSONTextWriter.WriteValue(' '+saleinvoiceline.Description+' '+saleinvoiceline."Unit of Measure Code"+' '+FORMAT(saleinvoiceline.Quantity*1.0)+' '
            +FORMAT(ROUND((saleinvoiceline."Unit Price"), 0.0001, '>')*1.0)+'.0000'+' '+FORMAT(saleinvoiceline."Line Discount Amount")+'.0000'+
            ' '+FORMAT((saleinvoiceline."Amount Including VAT"))+'.0000');
          UNTIL saleinvoiceline.NEXT=0;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            REPEAT
             IF GLAccount.GET(saleinvoiceline."No.") THEN
             HSCode2 := GLAccount."HS Codes";
            IF HSCode2 <> '' THEN
            JSONTextWriter.WriteValue(' '+saleinvoiceline.Description+' '+saleinvoiceline."Unit of Measure Code"+' '+FORMAT(saleinvoiceline.Quantity)+' '
            +FORMAT(saleinvoiceline."Unit Price")+' '+FORMAT(saleinvoiceline."Line Amount" ) );
          UNTIL saleinvoiceline.NEXT=0;
            END;


        {
        JSONTextWriter.WriteValue(' FLOUR WHEAT EXE 2KG THIS IS A 1.50 50.00 75.00');
        JSONTextWriter.WriteValue(' SUGAR NZOIA 50KG 1.00 100.00 100.00');
        JSONTextWriter.WriteValue('0001.13.09 SPIRIT TYPE JET FUEL 1.00 19.50 19.50');
        JSONTextWriter.WriteValue('0039.11.16 SOME ZERO RATED ITEM 1.00 15.00 15.00');
        JSONTextWriter.WriteValue('0001.11.00 BOVINE SEMEN EXEMPT ITEM 1.00 10.00 10.00');
        }

      JSONTextWriter.WriteEndArray;
         {
         saleinvoiceline.CALCSUMS("Line Discount Amount");
         CreateJsonAttribute('net_discount_total',saleinvoiceline."Line Discount Amount");
         CreateJsonAttribute('net_subtotal',salesinvoice.Amount);
         }
      END;
      JSONTextWriter.WriteEndObject;
      JsonOut:=StringBuilder.ToString;
      variables:=JsonOut;





       fnPostSign(variables,invoice_number,cu_serial_number,cu_invoice_number,verify_url, kradevices."Base ip address");
       // MESSAGE (cu_serial_number);



        IF cu_serial_number<>'' THEN
        AddSigned(invoice_number,cu_serial_number, cu_invoice_number, verify_url, KRAPrintLog);
        END;
        END;

          // END;
      //End get invoice




      //END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateJsonAttribute@100000010(Attributename@1000 : Text;Value@1001 : Variant);
    VAR
      JSONTextWriter@1003 : DotNet "'Newtonsoft.Json, Version=6.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=30ad4fe6b2a6aeed'.Newtonsoft.Json.JsonTextWriter";
      JSON@1002 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.String";
    BEGIN
      JSONTextWriter.WritePropertyName(Attributename);
      JSONTextWriter.WriteValue(FORMAT(Value));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE fnPostSign@7(variables@1004 : Text;VAR invoice_number@1003 : Code[100];VAR cu_serial_number@1002 : Code[100];VAR cu_invoice_number@1001 : Code[100];VAR verify_url@1000 : Text;baseip@1018 : Text) ResponseData : Text;
    VAR
      url@1017 : Text;
      Request@1016 : DotNet "'System, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.HttpWebRequest";
      WebResponse@1015 : DotNet "'System, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Net.HttpWebResponse";
      StreamReader@1014 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.IO.StreamReader";

      StreamWriter@1011 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.IO.StreamWriter";
      httpWebRequest@1010 : Codeunit 1297;
      JsonOut@1009 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.String";
      JsonConvert@1008 : DotNet "'Newtonsoft.Json, Version=6.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=30ad4fe6b2a6aeed'.Newtonsoft.Json.JsonConvert";
      JToken@1007 : DotNet "'Newtonsoft.Json, Version=6.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=30ad4fe6b2a6aeed'.Newtonsoft.Json.Linq.JToken";
      JObject@1006 : DotNet "'Newtonsoft.Json, Version=6.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=30ad4fe6b2a6aeed'.Newtonsoft.Json.Linq.JObject";
      JValue@1005 : DotNet "'Newtonsoft.Json, Version=6.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=30ad4fe6b2a6aeed'.Newtonsoft.Json.Linq.JValue";
    BEGIN
      url:=baseip+'?invoice+2';
      Request := Request.HttpWebRequest.Create(url);
      Request.Method := 'POST';
      Request.ContentType := 'application/json';
      Request.Headers.Add('Authorization', 'Basic ZxZoaZMUQbUJDljA7kTExQ==');
      StreamWriter := StreamWriter.StreamWriter(Request.GetRequestStream);
      StreamWriter.Write(variables);
      StreamWriter.Close;
      StreamWriter.Dispose;
      WebResponse := Request.GetResponse();

      StreamReader := StreamReader.StreamReader(WebResponse.GetResponseStream);
      ResponseData := StreamReader.ReadToEnd;


      IF ResponseData<>'' THEN BEGIN
        ResponseData:=CONVERTSTR(ResponseData, '\', ' ');
      JToken:=JToken.Parse(ResponseData);
      {
      MESSAGE(FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('invoice_number')));
      MESSAGE(FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('cu_serial_number')));
      MESSAGE(FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('cu_invoice_number')));
      MESSAGE(FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('verify_url')));
      MESSAGE(FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('description')));
      }
      invoice_number:=FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('invoice_number'));
      cu_invoice_number:=FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('cu_invoice_number'));
      cu_serial_number:=FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('cu_serial_number'));
      verify_url:=FORMAT(JToken.SelectToken('verify_url'));
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AddSigned@17(invoice_number@1004 : Code[100];cu_serial_number@1003 : Code[100];cu_invoice_number@1002 : Code[100];verify_url@1001 : Text;KRAPrintLog@1000 : Record 99999);
    VAR
      TempBlob@1007 : Record 99008535;
      QRCodeInput@1006 : Text;
      QRCodeFileName@1005 : Text;
    BEGIN
      CreateQRCode(DELCHR(verify_url,'=',' ') ,TempBlob);
      KRAPrintLog.INIT;
      KRAPrintLog .QrCode:=TempBlob.Blob;
      KRAPrintLog.cu_invoicenumber:=cu_invoice_number;
      KRAPrintLog.cu_serialnumber:=cu_serial_number;
      KRAPrintLog."Document No":=invoice_number;
      KRAPrintLog.INSERT;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateQRCode@1020089(QRCodeInput@1020047 : Text[250];VAR TempBLOB@1020048 : Record 99008535);
    VAR
      QRCodeFileName@1020049 : Text[1024];
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(TempBLOB);
      QRCodeFileName := GetQRCode(QRCodeInput);
      UploadFileBLOBImportandDeleteServerFile(TempBLOB,QRCodeFileName);
    END;

    PROCEDURE UploadFileBLOBImportandDeleteServerFile@1020098(VAR TempBlob@1020048 : Record 99008535;FileName@1020049 : Text[1024]);
    VAR
      FileManagement@33027920 : Codeunit 419;
    BEGIN
      FileName := FileManagement.UploadFileSilent(FileName);
      FileManagement.BLOBImportFromServerFile(TempBlob,FileName);

      DeleteServerFile(FileName);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DeleteServerFile@1020047(ServerFileName@1020000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      IF ERASE(ServerFileName) THEN;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetQRCode@1020038(QRCodeInput@1020001 : Text[250]) QRCodeFileName : Text[1024];
    VAR
      IBarCodeProvider@1020000 : DotNet "'Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.MX, Version=10.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.MX.BarcodeProviders.IBarcodeProvider";
    BEGIN
      GetBarCodeProvider(IBarCodeProvider);
      QRCodeFileName := IBarCodeProvider.GetBarcode(QRCodeInput);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetBarCodeProvider@1020001(VAR IBarCodeProvider@1020000 : DotNet "'Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.MX, Version=10.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.MX.BarcodeProviders.IBarcodeProvider" RUNONCLIENT);
    VAR
      QRCodeProvider@1020002 : DotNet "'Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.MX, Version=10.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.MX.BarcodeProviders.QRCodeProvider" RUNONCLIENT;
    BEGIN
      IF ISNULL(IBarCodeProvider) THEN
        IBarCodeProvider := QRCodeProvider.QRCodeProvider;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE invoiceEmail@18(invoiceNumber@1000 : Code[50]);
    VAR
      SMTPMailSetup@1001 : Record 409;
      SMTPMail@1002 : Codeunit 400;
      EmailID@1003 : Text;
      SalesInvoiceHeader@1004 : Record 112;
      SelesInvoieHeaderTemplate@1005 : TEMPORARY Record 112;
      SalesInvoice@1006 : Report 54031;
      TempFileName@1007 : Text;
      IStraeam@1008 : InStream;
      OStream@1009 : OutStream;
      XmlParameters@1010 : Text;
      cust@1011 : Record 18;
    BEGIN
      SMTPMailSetup.GET;

      SalesInvoiceHeader.RESET;
      SalesInvoiceHeader.SETRANGE("No.", invoiceNumber);
      IF SalesInvoiceHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      IF cust.GET(SalesInvoiceHeader."Sell-to Customer No.") THEN BEGIN

      EmailID:=cust."E-Mail";
      IF EmailID<>'' THEN BEGIN
      SalesInvoice .SETTABLEVIEW(SalesInvoiceHeader);
      XmlParameters:=SalesInvoice .RUNREQUESTPAGE();
      //SelesInvoieHeaderTemplate.Parameters.CREATEOUTSTREAM(OStream,TEXTENCODING::UTF8);
      //SelesInvoieHeaderTemplate.Parameters.CREATEINSTREAM(IStream,TEXTENCODING::UTF8);
      REPORT.SAVEAS(54031,'',REPORTFORMAT::Pdf,OStream);

      CLEAR(SMTPMail);
      SMTPMail.CreateMessage('',SMTPMailSetup."User ID",EmailID,'Invoice','',TRUE);
      SMTPMail.AddAttachmentStream(IStraeam,'Ivoice'+ SalesInvoiceHeader."No."+'.pdf');
      SMTPMail.AppendBody('Hi '+cust.Name+',');

      SMTPMail.AppendBody('<br>');
      SMTPMail.AppendBody('Please find attached your Customer Invoice');
      SMTPMail.AppendBody('<FIN>');
      SMTPMail.AppendBody('This is a system generated mail. Please do not reply to this mail!');
      SMTPMail.Send;
      //MESSAGE(Mail sent to Customer %1,Custno);
      END;
      END;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
